| Group | Count | % | Target |
|-------|-------|---|--------|
| White / Western European | 232 | 45% | 44% |
| East Asian | 96 | 18% | 19% |

| Black / African | 56 | 11% | 11% |
| South Asian | 37 | 7% | 7% |
| Middle Eastern / MENA | 21 | 4% | 4% |
| Southeast Asian | 10 | 2% | 2% |

## Gender: 337 male (65%)  ·  184 female (35%)  target 65/35%

### 1 · The Architect
